var filesToLoad = [];

// Do cutting-the-mustard

var supportsAsyncScriptLoading = true;
var script = document.createElement('script');
if (typeof script.async === 'undefined') {
  // Not supported
  supportsAsyncScriptLoading = false;
} else if (script.async !== true) {
  // Script execution order not supported (Safari 5.0)
  supportsAsyncScriptLoading = false;
}

var supportsAjax =
  typeof new XMLHttpRequest().onreadystatechange !== 'undefined';
if (
  Number(window.svt.nyh.featureToggles.TOGGLE_FORCE_BAREBONES) === 1 ||
  !window.Modernizr.cors ||
  !window.Modernizr.history ||
  !supportsAjax ||
  !supportsAsyncScriptLoading ||
  window.svt.oldIE
) {
  // Cut the mustard to barebones!
  filesToLoad.push(window.svt.nyh.scriptUrls.barebones);
} else {
  // Run full app!
  filesToLoad.push(window.svt.nyh.scriptUrls.vendor);
  filesToLoad.push(window.svt.nyh.scriptUrls.application);
}

// Load correct file(s)

for (var i = 0; i < filesToLoad.length; i += 1) {
  script = document.createElement('script');
  script.src = filesToLoad[i];
  if (supportsAsyncScriptLoading) {
    // async=false still downloads async since this is dynamically added, but
    // still guarantees execution-order:
    // https://www.html5rocks.com/en/tutorials/speed/script-loading/
    script.async = false;
  }
  document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);
}

</script>
